        function setCustomDimensions() {
            // Use set to persist page type so it is sent in all subsequent GA calls
            ga('set', 'dimension6', getPageType());  
  
            setTimeout(function() {
                if(getCookie("isUserRegistered")) {
                    var registrationStatus= getCookie("isUserRegistered");
                    if(registrationStatus === "true") {
                        ga('set', 'dimension1', 'Registered');
                    }
                } else {
                    ga('set', 'dimension1', 'Unregistered');
                }

                if(getCookie("isUserSubscribed")) {
                    var subscribedStatus= getCookie("isUserSubscribed")
                    if(subscribedStatus === "true") {
                        ga('set', 'dimension2', 'Subscribed');

        ga('provide', 'determineBreakingNews', function(tracker) {
            // Dimension7: Is the first Top Story teaser tagged as a "Major Story" or just a "Standard Teaser"?
            var firstTopStoryTagsArray;
    
            try {
                firstTopStoryTagsArray = sinclairDigital.facade.content['page-data'].teaser[0].teasers[0].tags;
            } catch(e) {
                firstTopStoryTagsArray = [];
            }
    
            var isBreakingNewsPresentInFirstPosition = false;
            if (firstTopStoryTagsArray) { // could be null, if .tags is null (no tags provided)
                firstTopStoryTagsArray.forEach(function (tagData) {
                    if (tagData["dimension"] === "Display" && tagData["name"] === "Major Story") {
                        isBreakingNewsPresentInFirstPosition = true;
                    }
                });
            }
    
            sinclairDigitalAnalytics.customDimensions.dimension7 =
                isBreakingNewsPresentInFirstPosition
                    ? "major-story-teaser"
                    : "standard-teaser";
        });

class="StoryTags-module_listTagWrapper__hA5o"><p class="StoryTags-module_para__pyQi">TOPICS:</p><a class="StoryTags-module_storyTag__jAYb" data-index="0" data-tag-name="Hepatitis A" draggable="true" class="StoryTags-module_storyTag__jAYb" data-index="2" data-tag-name="Homeless" draggable="true" href="/topic/Homeless">Homeless</a><a class="StoryTags-module_storyTag__jAYb" data-index="3" href="/topic/Maine%20CDC">Maine CDC</a><a class="StoryTags-module_storyTag__jAYb" data-index="5" data-tag-name="Encampments" draggable="true" href="/topic/Encampments">Encampments</a><a data-tag-name="Contaminated" draggable="true" href="/topic/Contaminated">Contaminated</a></ul></div><div class="StoryTags-module_tagWrapperLine__Jfav"></div><div class="StoryText-module_storyText__FWhP"><p>PORTLAND (WGME) -- Hepatitis A, which is highly infectious, is spreading through homeless encampments in Portland, according to the Press Herald. More than a dozen people have reportedly been<span class="extraSpace"></span>infected in the past few months.</p><p>As of Nov. 20, there have been 18 confirmed hepatitis A cases in Portland, according to Maine CDC.<span class="extraSpace"></span></p><p>According to the Maine CDC,<span class="extraSpace"></span> an outbreak is defined as three or more cases of a disease that are linked.</p><ul><li><strong>Also read: <a href="https://wgme.com/news/local/another-restaurant-worker-tests-positive-for-hepatitis-a-heres-what-you-should-know-about-the-disease" target="_blank" title="https://wgme.com/news/local/another-restaurant-worker-tests-positive-for-hepatitis-a-heres-what-you-should-know-about-the-disease" class="themeColorForLinks">Another restaurant worker tests positive for hepatitis A, here's what you should know about the disease</a></strong></li></ul><p>According to the Press Herald, most of the cases have been detected in the homeless community.<span class="extraSpace"></span> However, one case was diagnosed in an employee at the Green Elephant Bistro in Portland.</p><p>Three cases have also been reported in Androscoggin County.</p><p></p><p>An employee at Marcos Italian Restaurant in Lewiston and an employee at Dockside Grill in Falmouth were also diagnosed with hepatitis A over the past two months.<br></p><p>Advocates for the homeless to the Press Herald that the outbreak stems from a lack of access to clean water for drinking and bathing.<br></p><p>Hepatitis A is a contagious liver disease. It can spread through person-to-person contact or by consuming contaminated food or water.</p><p>Health concerns have been cited by Portland officials as a reason for clearing out camps.<span class="extraSpace"></span></p><ul><li><strong>Also read: <a href="https://wgme.com/news/local/worker-at-portland-vegetarian-restaurant-tests-positive-for-hepatitis-a" target="_blank" title="https://wgme.com/news/local/worker-at-portland-vegetarian-restaurant-tests-positive-for-hepatitis-a" class="themeColorForLinks">Worker at Portland vegetarian restaurant tests positive for hepatitis A</a></strong></li></ul><p>An infected person can spread the virus to others from about two weeks before symptom onset until one week after symptoms begin, according to the Maine CDC.</p><p>You can prevent getting hepatitis A with a vaccine. People exposed to hepatitis A can avoid getting sick if they get the vaccine within 14 days of the exposure.</p><p><strong><em>This story will be updated.</em></strong></p></div></div></div></div><div
